Summary of the Newly Compiled Catalog of the Song Dynasty Tripitaka 114

The Song Dynasty Tripitaka, carved at Zhaisha and reprinted by the local Scripture Repository, has long been published. Its catalog, due to various connections within the entire collection, has only recently been published. The content is complete. Key points include: (1) Discrepancies in the Catalog: The catalog of Zhaisha in the Japanese Showa Buddhist Treasure contains many discrepancies and omissions compared to the actual scriptures currently found by the repository. Therefore, a new catalog has been compiled based on the actual scriptures, with the old Showa catalog attached for comparison. (2) Excellence of Various Monographs: Ye Gongchao's Small Chronicle of Yansheng Temple focuses on the history of the Zhaisha carvings, examining and annotating dozens of ancient books to form a system. Jiang Weiqiao's Record of the Beginning and End of the Ning Tripitaka Reprint describes the fundraising and operational situation, the difficulties encountered, and the care taken. (3) Treasures of the Prefaces: Traditionally, prefaces to scripture carvings focus on theoretical elaborations, but Zhu Qinglan's preface provides detailed historical accounts, and Wu Jiya's preface sincerely narrates the promotion. Both can be read as summaries. In addition, examples and page-filling tables are also related to textual research on the entire collection. With the publication of this record, the quality and value of the Zhaisha Tripitaka can be better represented. The repository has already sold out its existing collection. In order to meet the continued purchase requests from afar, it has negotiated with existing customers to relinquish ten copies, which will continue to be offered at the pre-agreed price of 525 yuan per copy as a preferential circulation (still at 712 Weihaiwei Road, Shanghai) for one month, after which it will be closed. It is said that the total cost of completing this project was over twenty thousand yuan, which was covered by Zhu and Ye.

Gao Wensheng Asleep: Man Attacks with a Knife; Guard Hears the Sound and Arrests Him; Identified as the Assailant 115

Gao Wensheng, 42 years old, a mud worker from Pudong, lived upstairs in the Hanji Clothing Store on Guizhou Road. At approximately 1:30 AM yesterday, while Gao was sleeping, a man suddenly rushed into his room with a sharp knife and slashed Gao's face and back twice. Bleeding profusely, Gao woke up in agony and screamed for help in the room. Nearby guards heard the commotion and rushed to investigate, seeing a man hurrying out the door, attempting to flee. They immediately arrested him. After Gao Wensheng identified him as the assailant, he was taken to the police station. Gao was taken to the hospital for treatment. It is reported that the motive for the attack was a love triangle.

South Huangpu Smuggling and Murder Case 116

Liu Heshang, a junzi boatman, loaded 200 piculs of junzi at Jiaxing to be delivered to a certain Japanese firm in Shanghai. Yesterday morning at approximately 5:00 AM, while sailing at a location 18 li long in the South Huangpu, four small boats suddenly approached, and over ten bandits armed with broadswords, iron rulers, and wooden sticks jumped out. Four of the bandits, wearing gray clothes and pants, swarmed forward, beat Liu, and forced him to hand over money. When he replied that he had no money, they tied him up on the boat. The four or five crew members, seeing the fierce situation, did not dare to resist. The bandits searched the cabin, robbing over 50 yuan in national currency and all the clothes of the crew members. Still unsatisfied, they carried away over ten piculs of junzi before fleeing. Yesterday afternoon at approximately 6:00 PM, they arrived in Shanghai. Liu was seriously injured and died before receiving medical treatment. Two other crew members were also beaten and injured and are currently being treated in the hospital. The robbery has been reported to the cargo owner.

Cattle and Sheep Prices Suddenly Rise: Public Association to Convene Meeting to Discuss 120

Cattle and sheep prices in this city have risen by 20% due to the suspension of livestock shipments from Anhui and Liaoning provinces. As most of the cattle and sheep in the city are supplied by Liaoning, and Anhui province has suffered from drought and flood years, there is a shortage of draft cattle. Therefore, a notice has been issued to all counties to suspend exports in order to facilitate cultivation. As a result, cattle from Bengbu have been stopped from coming to Shanghai. The Liaoning-Ning area also banned the export of cattle and sheep at the beginning of the month. As a result, goods are scarce, and the market is feeling the strain of supply not meeting demand. It is estimated that the city's daily sales of cattle and sheep are about 6,000 heads, and these two provinces usually supply about 2,000 to 3,000 heads. Since the ban on shipments to Shanghai, although other provinces of Zhejiang and Jiangsu still have shipments to Shanghai, the shipments are rare, so the black market prices have risen by 20%. The Cattle and Sheep Industry Association plans to convene a meeting in the coming days to discuss the matter.

Dong Jiancheng, from Changzhou, residing at 51 Hongan Lane, Hanzhong Road, Zhabei, has an adopted daughter named Shuangda, 15 years old, short in stature, still developing, with cropped hair, and due to a past measles outbreak, her eyes seem to be tearing. Letter 131

To the Editor,

Having recently read the local news section of your esteemed newspaper, which contained a news item stating: "The treatment of thirteen fish dealers after entering the fish market was not resolved yesterday." There are inconsistencies regarding the service fee, with the market collecting one-quarter of the proceeds. The actual service fee is 2%, and other rights are the same as those of the eight existing businesses. This equal treatment was decided by the board of directors of the market yesterday and announced to the managers of the thirteen businesses. It is believed that your newspaper's report on this matter was due to a misunderstanding of the rumors. We are writing to request that you correct it.

Sincerely,

Aquatic Fresh Fish Industry Association

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather around Shandong and the lower reaches of the Yangtze River would change from obstructed to cloudy, but it would still be sunny. There would be a light northeast to southeast wind. The weather in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River would be cloudy, with rain or fog in several places. The weather in the East China Sea and Taiwan would be cloudy, with rain or fog, and a light northeast to southeast wind. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 82.4 degrees, and the lowest was 65.3 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 90.1 degrees, and the lowest was 65.8 degrees.

Education News

President Chiang Instructs the Ministry of Education to Intensify Training of Primary and Secondary School Teachers. Summer Courses to Be Established in Various Provinces and Cities This Year. Designated Schools to Conduct Training for Teachers of Various Subjects. 133

(Nanjing, 6th) President Chiang recently instructed the Ministry of Education regarding the professional development of primary and secondary school teachers, emphasizing that improving the teaching staff should be considered a primary task of educational administration going forward. After detailed planning, the Ministry of Education has determined standards and will implement fundamental methods to address the issue. This involves strictly urging secondary schools and above to intensify mental, disciplinary, and other fundamental training in accordance with the prescribed special education plans, in order to cultivate talent. Remedial measures involve providing supplementary training to current teachers, giving them opportunities for further education and remedial learning. These training sessions can be organized directly by the central government, or, due to the large number of trainees, they can be organized separately by provinces and cities, utilizing the scientific facilities and personnel of excellent local universities. It is reported that the Ministry of Education has decided on the following implementation measures: (1) Order all provinces and cities, starting this year, to take advantage of secondary school summer vacations to organize primary school teacher training sessions by district, or to entrust normal schools to handle them, or to assign the local responsible educational administrative organs to organize them, so that all primary school teachers under their jurisdiction will have the opportunity to participate in at least one training session within the next three years. (2) Order the education departments and bureaus of each province and city to jointly establish teacher training courses for secondary schools with excellent local universities designated by the Ministry of Education, divided into subjects such as mathematics, science, history, geography, and English. The departments and bureaus of each province and city will formulate a plan for the rotation of teachers of various subjects in secondary schools throughout the province and city, so that all teachers of various subjects in secondary schools will have the opportunity to participate in at least one training session within three years. The designated universities are: National Central, Peking, Tsinghua, Peking Normal, Wuhan, Sun Yat-sen, Zhejiang, Jiaotong, Shandong, and Sichuan (national universities); Guangxi and Hunan (provincial universities); and Jinling, Huazhong, Datong, Hujiang, and Xiamen (private universities). (3) The Ministry of Education will jointly prepare the summer training sessions for teachers of agricultural vocational schools with the Central Agricultural College, divided into agronomy (crop and sericulture groups). Domestic agricultural experts will be lecturers. Each public and private agricultural vocational school in each province and city will select one to two full-time teachers to participate in the training, to improve their knowledge and skills in agricultural teaching. The training period will be five weeks, and the training location will be the Central Congress. (4) The Ministry of Education will entrust the Shanghai Private Lei Shi De Industrial Vocational School to organize the summer training sessions for teachers of industrial vocational schools, divided into three classes: mechanical, civil engineering, and applied chemistry. Each public and private industrial vocational school in each province and city will select one to two people to participate in the training, to improve their knowledge and skills in industrial teaching. The training time will be fifteen days. The above four items have all been implemented by the Ministry of Education. In addition, measures for short-term primary school teacher training and training of public education cadres are also being drafted for gradual implementation.

The City's Teachers Celebrate Teachers' Day Enthusiastically. Director Pan of the Education Bureau Attends and Gives Instructions. Please Request the Ministry of Education to Promulgate Teachers' Day. 136

Yesterday was Teachers' Day. The United Association of Teachers and Staff of Primary and Secondary Schools in this city held a celebration meeting at the auditorium of Minli Middle School in Dananmen at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, and a dinner party and social gathering in the evening. Details are recorded separately below.

Participating Teachers. More than 500 teachers and staff from major primary and secondary schools attended, including Mayor Wu (represented by Hongda), Director Pan, Chen Gongsu, and Tong Hangbai. Jiang Jianbai, Liu Zhun-en, Chen Jicheng, Xu Zexiang, Tao Guangchuan, Yan Zhenyu, Zhao Shusheng, Cui Jianwu, Feng Yixian, Xu Shushen, Wu Ziqian, and Ma Zhen served as the presidium. Sun Yucai recorded, Zhang Xiaotian served as the master of ceremonies, and Luo Bian and Yuan Dingchang were responsible for reception. After the ceremony was performed as usual, the chairman Liu Zhun-en delivered a speech, and Jiang Jianbai reported on the preparation process. Next, Mayor Wu and Director Pan were invited to give instructions, and Chen Gongsu and others gave speeches. Finally, proposals were passed, photos were taken, and the meeting adjourned.

Chairman's Speech. Liu Zhun-en, Chairman of the Presidium, stated in his speech that this year's Teachers' Day is different from previous years. During this period of national crisis, how to implement national crisis education and promote national salvation is the current priority. First, there should be a spirit of struggle. Teachers themselves must work harder. Second, there should be a spirit of unity. Teachers should unite to carry out the national salvation movement. Third, there should be a spirit of sacrifice, preparing to sacrifice for the country and the nation. I hope that our teachers will fight to the end. Next, Jiang Jianbai reported on the preparation process, explaining the points of this year's Teachers' Day and the responsibilities of teachers.

Director's Instructions. Following Mayor Wu's speech, Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau was invited to give instructions, stating that Teachers' Day is not only for celebration, but also for happiness, especially in times of national crisis. Teachers in general should be more excited, self-respecting, and confident. Our only leader, Chairman Chiang, has mentioned education in his speeches and writings these past few years, and has always regarded education as the most important thing. Therefore, we always believe that only education can save the country. We should respect ourselves, respect ourselves, and work tirelessly. If the hundreds of thousands of teachers in the country all have this concept of self-respect and self-respect to motivate all initiative, then the country's revival will surely achieve excellent results. Secondly, we should follow this ten-year summary of life, ten-year lessons, and the famous dictum that "what Heaven imparts is called nature; to follow one's nature is called the Way; to cultivate the Way is called education" as the standard for our teachers' self-cultivation. Next, Chen Gong delivered a speech.

Proposals Passed. Next, the proposals were passed: (1) Petitioning the Ministry of Education to issue an order stipulating June 6 as Teachers' Day, in order to celebrate it, (2) Petitioning the Ministry of Education to order bookstores to reduce the prices of textbooks to reduce the burden and facilitate popularization, and (3) Organizing a joint office of the United Association of Teachers and Staff of Primary and Secondary Schools in this city, with Chen Jicheng, Jiang Jianbai, Feng Yixian, Sun Yucai and others exchanging opinions before making a decision. After the meeting adjourned, a dinner party and social gathering was held at Minli Middle School.

Zheng Zhaolin was publicly elected as Chairman, reporting on the preparation process. Subsequently, Zhou Xiangxian, Zhu Kezhen, Xu Shaodi, and others delivered speeches, generally stating that teachers bear a significant responsibility to society and must pay special attention to and cultivate children's physical and intellectual abilities. Afterwards, two proposals were passed: (1) To request the Ministry of Education, in conjunction with the Examination Yuan and the Ministry of Personnel, to establish regulations for awarding honors to educational service personnel, to be promulgated by the state, thereby providing spiritual rewards for those who have served diligently and contributed to education. (2) To request the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Department of Education to allow middle school teachers to pursue one year of advanced studies at a national university after five years of teaching, to refresh their knowledge. Recreational activities were also held to foster interest. The meeting adjourned at 12 PM.

Huaiyuan: (Central News Agency, Qingjiangpu, 6th) Due to the ongoing national crisis, primary and secondary schools in Huaiyuan did not have a holiday for Teacher's Day but instead held gatherings after class.

Guangzhou: (Hong Kong, 6th) Over a thousand teachers in the city did not hold a grand Teacher's Day commemoration meeting on the 6th.

Kaifeng: (Kaifeng, 6th) A Teacher's Day commemoration meeting was held at the Dalu Cinema on the morning of the 6th. Schools were given a one-day holiday. Over thirty faculty and staff members attended. Li Lianfang presided over the meeting.

Dispute at Xiamen University 138

(Xiamen, 6th) Due to a decrease in students and financial difficulties, the Xiamen University board decided to reduce departments and merge faculties in the next academic year. Students from the Faculty of Education formed a "Faculty Protection Association" to oppose this decision, but without success. On the 6th, a university-wide student meeting resolved to send a telegram to the Ministry of Education, requesting that the university be taken over by the state. A telegram was also sent to Chen Jiageng explaining the reasons. News followed of Chen's resignation as Chairman of the Board and Lin Wenqing's resignation as President of the University.

Number of National Higher Education Faculty and Staff in the 23rd Year 141

In June of this year, the Ministry of Education conducted a statistical survey of the number of faculty and staff in national vocational schools and above (including vocational schools, independent colleges, and universities) in the 23rd year. An abstract is provided below:

In the 23rd year, faculty and staff in national vocational schools and above are divided into three categories: full-time, part-time within the school, and part-time outside the school. (1) There are 3,141 full-time faculty members and 4,113 full-time staff members, totaling 7,254 full-time faculty and staff members, accounting for 68.60% of the total number of faculty and staff. (2) There are 1,100 faculty members and 1,100 staff members who are part-time within the school. Faculty and staff members who hold multiple positions are counted as one person, totaling 1,100, accounting for 10.40%. (4) There are 2,079 faculty members and 141 staff members who are part-time outside the school, totaling 2,220 faculty and staff members, accounting for over 21%. In total, there are 10,574 faculty and staff members across the three categories. If faculty and staff are counted separately, the total number of faculty members across the three categories (full-time and part-time) is 6,320, and the total number of staff members across the three categories (full-time and part-time) is 5,354. In terms of percentages, for faculty members, full-time accounts for 49.7%, part-time within the school accounts for 17.41%, and part-time outside the school accounts for 32.89%. For staff members, full-time accounts for 76.82%, part-time within the school accounts for 20.5%, and part-time outside the school accounts for 2.63%.

Short Distance Trials 147

Our participation in the World Games track and field preliminary selection, scheduled to be held at Shenyuan this afternoon at 2:00 PM for the Sino-Western competition, was preceded by trials at Shenyuan yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM due to the large number of participants in the sprint events and the lack of accurate results. As a result, Fu Jincheng and Cheng Jinguan were selected for the 100 meters, Cheng Jinguan for the 200 meters, and Li Yanxiang for the 400 meters. All details are as follows:

100 Meters: The participants in the 100-meter trials included Fu Jincheng, Cheng Jinguan, Zhang Xikui, Ye Songping, Chen Yongfu, and Yan Zhaoshen. After the lanes were drawn, everyone except Cheng Jinguan false-started three times. Because it was a trial, it was still allowed to continue. After the start, Fu Jincheng took the lead, followed by Cheng Jinguan, and the rest were behind. At 80 meters, Zhang Xikui accelerated, almost equaling Cheng Jinguan, but fortunately, Cheng had a strong sprint and maintained second place. Fu Jincheng crossed the line first, with a distance of about three feet, and a time of eleven seconds.

400 Meters: Only Li Yanxiang, Zhu Aixian, and Chen Mingliang participated in the 400 meters. After the start, everyone was very close, with almost no distinction between them. At about 130 meters from the finish line, Zhu Aixian accelerated, pushing forward desperately, but it was a flash in the pan and soon became weak again. Li Yanxiang, on the other hand, ran tighter and tighter, reaching the finish line first with a time of 53.6 seconds, followed by Zhu with a time of 54.1 seconds, and Chen Mingliang in third, with poor posture and running very hard.

200 Meters: The participants in the 200-meter trials included Cheng Jinguan, Ye Songping, and Yan Zhaoshen. Cheng started very quickly and took the lead throughout, with an increasingly powerful sprint to the end. The others were far behind. Cheng reached the finish line first with a time of 23 seconds, leading by about three meters. Ye Songping and Yan Zhaoshen finished second and third, with a difference of one meter between them.

100 Meters: (1) Fu Jincheng, (2) Cheng Jinguan, (3) Zhang Xikui, 11 seconds.

200 Meters: (1) Cheng Jinguan, (2) Ye Songping, (3) Yan Zhaoshen, 23 seconds.

400 Meters: (1) Li Yanxiang, (2) Zhu Aixian, (3) Chen Mingliang, 53.6 seconds.

Jiangda Football: Guanghua Champion; Beats Jinan 1-0; Seven-Year Championship Changes Hands 152

After Jinan and Guanghua both ranked first with three points in Jiangda football, according to the association's regulations, the finals were held at the City Sports Stadium yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. As a result, Guanghua scored a goal by Jiang Zhaoxiang under the threat of the enemy, and won this year's championship 1-0. Jiangda football then came to an end. According to the tournament, which began in 1915 of the Republic of China and has now reached its tenth edition, Jinan has maintained it for seven consecutive years except for the first edition which was won by Fudan, and the second edition which was equally divided between Guanghua, Jinan, and Jiaotong University. This year it was finally taken by Guanghua. At the same time, Jiangda's six championship matches for this year also came to an end.

Yesterday, the gold market saw a rebound in London spot gold, sluggish selling pressure, and major players such as Chun Yuan Yong buying aggressively. In addition, Da Decheng and others also covered short positions, gradually breaking through the 40 yuan barrier. Early in the morning, overseas silver markets saw flat prices in both England and America. Floor traders said that the market was weak after the close and that there were sellers offering prices lower than 0.0625. Monterey forward silver prices narrowed from one to one and seven tenths of a penny. England and America were both flat. London spot gold rose three pence. The Central Bank announced its exchange rates, with England and America both flat. Customs gold units rose four li. Spot gold prices were quoted at 1126 yuan and six yuan. Pre-market trading opened higher at around 37 yuan, with Qiafeng, Yongfu, Taiheng, Dingkang, and Chun Yuan Yong all buying. After rising to above eight yuan, the market opened high. After the opening, there were multiple positions, and HSBC Bank announced its exchange rates, with England and America both flat. The market hovered around eight yuan, and the multiple parties sold some positions, leading to a slight setback. However, Chun Yuan Yong and others took the opportunity to aggressively buy, allowing the price to rise again. Children's Special

Determination 171

— Wanwen

Little friends! Before I talk about determination, I must first analyze it. "Decision" means to decide, and "heart" is the heart in the human body. The meaning of "decision" is to decide with your heart. In fact, how can the heart decide? This is all the work of the brain, but it is a common saying. I will follow this saying to talk about determination.

The words "determination" sound very familiar. Looking at them seems ordinary. Why did I write about it? Because determination is the main condition for promoting the success of a career. I will give a few examples to prove it. Inventors made a determination before inventing various things that benefit the world. Dr. Sun Yat-sen made a determination before there was the Republic of China. Their success was of course caused by various reasons, but determination is also one of them. If you want to do something, and your mind is hesitant, listening to this person saying to do it and that person saying not to do it, then this thing will never succeed. In short, when a person is alive, he must have determination in everything he does.

However, if determination is used inappropriately, not only will it not be beneficial, but it will be harmful. Therefore, when you want to do something, use your mind to judge whether you want to be determined or not. I said earlier, "You must have determination in everything you do," but now I say, "You must judge the application of determination." Don't you all think this is contradictory? Let me explain it now. Everything has good and bad aspects, and good and bad have no fixed standard. Use your judgment to decide if this matter is beneficial, then resolve to do it. If it is useless, discard it. In this way, determination is your good friend, able to help you succeed in your career and get good results.

Child Prodigies 172

— Zhou Xian

A Ten-Year-Old Musician

In the village of Osde Tudde in the Vistula River basin in southern Poland, there is a farmer's son named Buglai Mountain, who is only ten and a half years old this year, but he can play the piano very well. His father is very poor, so he has been studying in a free school since he was seven years old, but he can only study for two or three hours a day. The rest of his time is spent in his father's small pasture. Listening to the cold breeze from the Baltic Sea attacking the trees of varying heights around the pasture, he feels a kind of indescribably pleasant melody. In the late spring weather, listening to the sounds of various birds chirping from near and far, he feels that it is full of musical meaning. From the age of eight, he asked his father to buy him a small violin, and he played along with the sounds of nature in the pasture. Although his playing has no score, the gentle tone often attracts neighbors to gather around and listen to him play. Therefore, he is even happier, forgetting the responsibility of the work his father gave him. After repeated warnings from his father, his interest in playing did not diminish, and his violin was finally destroyed by his father. But this news was soon learned by a pastor in the church, so he agreed with his father to teach him to play the piano. No matter what the tune, he can learn it as soon as he learns it, and the excellent technique shows that he is rich in musical talent. The old pastor was very happy and taught him wholeheartedly. Last Christmas, he took him to Lublin to perform publicly and raise relief funds for poor children. As a result, he obtained a lot of money. Recently, I heard that the pastor has筹有欵 for him and will send him to France for further study.

A Thirteen-Year-Old Painter

Outside the city of Valences, on the Rhone River in France, lives a very poor family. The head of the family is a widow near fifty years old, named Mrs. Meigen Lee. A family of five lives on a few dairy cows. Her husband was an unknown painter who left behind four minor children, and the situation was very bleak. But her third daughter, Maria, has loved to paint since she was a child, and often copies her father's works, which she finds very interesting. From the age of ten, she worked even harder on painting. At the age of eleven, she opened a solo exhibition in the city of Valences. She sold a painting of "Dusk in Valences" for 300 francs. A painting of "Beggar and Dog" sold for 150 francs. In the spring of 1935, she held a solo exhibition outside the city of Lyon. A painting of "Jesus on the Cross" was priced at 600 francs and was finally sold for 750 francs. Her painting skills were entirely self-taught, and she has never been instructed by a famous teacher. Now, a distant relative has volunteered to help her study in Paris. The future accomplishments of this talented female painter are bound to be limitless.

"Lateness" 173

— Tree

One day, Washington questioned his secretary why he was late. His secretary replied that it was because the clock at his house was slow. Washington said sternly, "Then you can buy a correct clock! If you don't do this, I will immediately hire someone else." From then on, his secretary did not dare to be late again.

Napoleon invited guests one night, and when it was time to take their seats, the generals had not yet arrived. He sat down to eat alone. When he had finished eating and was about to leave the table, he saw the generals coming in. He nodded to the generals and said, "Now the time to eat has passed. Please go back to your respective duties." The late generals withdrew with blushing faces.

Little friends! Have you ever been late to school? "Lateness" is a very bad habit that will cultivate your laziness. Little friends, if you have ever been late, please correct it from today onwards.

Zhi'er's New Discovery 174

— Luan Mujie

Zhi'er is De'er's older brother. He's probably only thirteen years old this year! He does seem to be a little smarter than ordinary people. You only need to see him staring and contemplating all day long with lively and sharp eyes to know that his mind is very deep.

These past few days, De'er has always seen Zhi'er staring at the sky, not knowing what he is doing, so De'er asked him suspiciously:

"Brother! What are you always looking at in the sky?"

"Okay, I'll tell you! I've recently discovered that watching clouds is really the best way to pass the time." Zhi'er replied to his younger brother with a smile.

"Why is watching clouds the best way to pass the time?"

"For example, in the morning you see the clouds are red, yellow, purple, and blue, but when you look at them again in the middle of the day, they're different. Every cloud is as white as snow, like sailboats sailing quickly. If you look closely, there are cows, horses, and people, but if you look again, everything is gone. Especially on rainy days, the sky is full of dark clouds, like countless dragons swimming around in them, which is really beautiful. Brother! Don't underestimate it, it is indeed much better than movies and dramas! If you don't believe me, you might as well try it!" Sure enough, within a few days, De'er also contracted his brother's癖了.

Little friends! You might as well try it too!

Fantasy 175

— Translated by Xiao Feizhang

If many oceans all became one ocean,

What a huge ocean that would be!

If many trees all became one tree,

What a huge tree that would be!

If many iron axes all became one iron axe,

What a huge iron axe that would be!

If many people all became one person,

What a huge person that would be!

If this huge person took this huge iron axe,

And chopped down this huge tree,

And let it fall into this huge ocean,

What a huge splash that would make!

What Time Is It? 176

— Lu Luo

——An Interesting World Time Difference Chart——

Bright sunlight shines on our Earth.

The Earth rotates from west to east. One rotation is a day. We clever humans have divided this rotation time into twenty-four hours. So, one rotation of the Earth is twenty-four hours, which is one day.

The part of the Earth that receives sunlight is bright, which we call daytime. Only part of the Earth receives sunlight; the other part does not. The area without sunlight is called nighttime.

Therefore, at the same moment on Earth, some places have the sun directly overhead, which is noon; some places have the sun setting, which is afternoon; some places have the sun just going down, which is dusk; some places have the sun just rising, which is morning; and some places have no sun and are completely dark, which is night.

When we are eating lunch, people in different parts of the world are either getting up and washing their faces; some are carrying their schoolbags to school; some have finished lunch and are already in class; some are finishing school for the evening; some are already eating dinner; some are going to bed; and some are dreaming sweet dreams in bed.

Why is there such a difference? It turns out that the Earth is a sphere, and the time in different places on Earth is based on the sun—when the sun is directly overhead, it is noon. We divide the Earth into 360 degrees, and dividing 360 degrees by 24 gives us exactly 15 degrees per unit. Therefore, as the sun shines on the Earth, there is a one-hour difference every 15 degrees. Using this method to calculate the time in different parts of the world, we find that:

If it is 9:00 AM in Shanghai, then it is: 8:00 AM in Singapore; 7:00 AM in Calcutta, India; 3:30 AM in Moscow; 1:00 AM in London; 8:00 PM in New York; 5:00 PM in San Francisco; 2:30 PM in Hawaii; and 10:30 AM in Tokyo, Japan.

How can we know the time difference in different parts of the world?

Now I have a very simple method to teach children. As long as the children use their hands and do it themselves, they can easily succeed, and they don't need to spend money to buy any tools or materials. Just ask the children to prepare:

A pair of scissors, a piece of cardboard (about one square foot in size), a brass paper fastener, and some glue.

Haven't you all seen the circular map attached to the front? This map is a miniature of the world map (it widens the portion of the Southern Hemisphere). Because it is centered on the North Pole, looking at all directions of the Earth from the North Pole, the shapes of the land and sea on the surface become flat and wide.

Children, cut out this map, following the circular line; after cutting it out, paste it on the cardboard and cut the cardboard into a circle as well. Then, cut out the small circular diagram in the lower right corner that shows day and night and time, and paste it on the cardboard, also cutting it into a circle. Don't use too much or too little glue; apply it evenly.

After cutting out these two circles, one large and one small, make a hole in the center of each circle, place the small circle on the North Pole of the map—that is, the center—and then insert a brass paper fastener through the holes, folding the legs of the fastener on the back of the map. In this way, the world time difference checker is complete.

Suppose you want to check what time it is in major cities around the world when it is noon in Shanghai. You only need to align the number 12 on the small dial with the meridian of Shanghai. Then you can see the time in different places: Tokyo is 1:30 PM; Brisbane is 2:10 PM; Fiji is a little before 4:00 PM; Hawaii is 5:30 PM; San Francisco is 8:00 PM; New York is 11:10 PM; Rio de Janeiro is a little after 1:00 AM; London is 4:00 AM; Rome is 5:00 AM; Moscow is 6:30 AM; and so on, checking back to Shanghai.

If you want to use noon in London as the standard to check the time in different parts of the world, you can also do it according to the above method to find out.

Okay, I'm done talking. Please get to work, kids! The order of doing it is:

First, find the tools and materials; second, do it according to the method; third, play according to the method. Fourth, after playing, think of ways to improve it, or invent a method that is more convenient, or other new and valuable things to play with.

Small Scientific Question

Why Do Bubbles Appear on the Water Surface When a Brick Is Thrown into It? 177

— Zi Xi

If we casually take a brick and throw it into the water, bubbles will appear on the surface of the water in an instant. What is the reason for this? I am afraid that not many children know about this. Let me explain it simply:

When an object is thrown into water, it floats if it is lighter than the same volume of water; it sinks if it is heavier than the same volume of water. At the same time, the weight lost by an object in water is equal to the weight of the water displaced. Then, when we throw a brick into the water, it naturally sinks because it is heavier than the same volume of water. As it sinks, the water in contact with it is squeezed and dispersed around it, temporarily leaving a gap in the middle. However, the density and specific gravity of the air are both less than that of water, so although the gap is full of air, the density of the water near it is greater than that of the air, naturally because of the effect of surface tension. Quickly, it will compete to fill the gap to maintain its horizontal level, and the air in the gap is forced to have nowhere to go, so it is surrounded by the water film part by part, and becomes many air pockets of different sizes, rising up and floating on the surface of the water, which becomes the bubbles we usually see. When the bubbles break, the air will disperse. If you don't believe me, you can try it right away.

Clock 178

— Bai Ying

Bao'er was a lazy child. He always overslept and was always late for school.

One day, the teacher hit his palm ten times. He was very angry and thought: It's the clock's fault, it runs too fast.

When he returned home, he turned the short hand of the clock back one space.

The next day, when he arrived at school, the first class had already ended. He was very surprised. He thought, isn't my clock only eight o'clock? How could a class have already been taught?

The teacher saw him and asked sternly:

"Why are you so late today?"

He cried and sobbed:

"I thought: As long as I slow down the clock at home, school will start later, but I didn't know..."

Developing Images on White Paper 179

— Bai Yi

Kids! Now let me tell you three ways to develop images on white paper:

Dissolve a few pieces of alum in water, dip a clean brush in this alum water and write words or draw pictures on Chinese paper. After it dries, there will be no trace on the paper. But if you drag this paper in clear water, the writing on it will immediately become transparent and appear.

Dip a brush in rice water and write on the paper, then put it in water with iodine (available in ordinary pharmacies), and your handwriting will appear blue on the paper.

Write words on paper with milk, and after it dries, it will be a blank piece of paper, but if you bake it over a fire, the yellow writing will be clearly visible.

Biography of a Righteous Dog (21) 180

— Xin Qing

Mrs.柯甘士 dared not say anything aloud, but when she waited until 老达士's coffin was buried, 小南洛 and 柏德希 left, she gave a small wreath to her daughter 小洛, asking her to respectfully send it to the grave. She only saw a dark earthen mound standing in the snow.

小南洛 and 柏德希 returned home very sadly. But that desolate and lonely small house could no longer give them the slightest comfort. 老达士 still had one month's rent unpaid when he died, but 小南洛 did not have a single copper coin left after burying his old grandfather. He went to beg the owner of the small house, who was a shoemaker. He always smoked and drank with the miller 柯甘士 on Sunday nights. He ignored 小南洛's begging. He was cruel and stingy, and had always loved money like his life. He took all the pots, kettles, sticks, and stones in the small house to pay off the rent he was owed, and immediately ordered 小南洛 to move out tomorrow.

The house was small and low, simply shapeless, but they had lived there for too long, and they were very reluctant to leave. They had always been very happy living here. Every summer, the house was covered with vines, and the bean flowers bloomed fragrantly, setting off the sun-drenched fields, making the scenery even more beautiful. Although they worked hard and endured the taste of poverty on weekdays, they were very satisfied and happy in their hearts. Every night, they would always run back to see the old man's welcoming smile.

That night, 小南洛 and 柏德希 sat in the dark all night, next to the cold and fireless fireplace, holding each other tightly to keep warm. They did not feel very cold, but their hearts seemed to be frozen.

Dawn broke, and the morning light filled the snow-white and frozen earth. It was the morning of Christmas Eve. 小南洛 shivered, hugged his only good friend 柏德希 tightly, and drops of hot tears dripped on 柏德希's forehead. He said in a low voice, "Let's go! 柏德希 - dear 柏德希! We never want to wait to be kicked out by the landlord, let's go ourselves first."

柏德希 originally had no opinion, only obeying the orders of its young master. The two of them walked out of this beloved small house sadly. They felt that anything worthless in the house was very precious and lovely. 柏德希 walked past his green cart with his head drooping: it was no longer his. This cart and many other things had to be used to pay off the rent owed, as well as the copper driving object, lying shiny in the snow. When 柏德希 saw these two treasures that he had depended on for life, he simply wanted to lie down next to them and die immediately, but its young master was still alive and needed it. It still had to cheer up and fight on.

They walked on the road to 盎凡尔 that they used to walk every day. It was not yet dawn, and the windows of the houses were still closed. There were only a few villagers on the road. They did not pay attention when 小南洛 and 柏德希 passed by. 小南洛 stopped in front of a house and looked inside earnestly: his old grandfather had always been enthusiastic about helping this family when he was alive.

He said timidly: "Please, can you give 柏德希 some breadcrumbs? It is old and has not eaten anything since yesterday afternoon." The woman in the house immediately closed the door and muttered something about how expensive wheat and rice were this year. Poor 小南洛 and 柏德希 had no choice but to walk forward weakly; they never begged for food from others again.
